All Pokemon Changes and Learnsets are listed below. If I may have missed something along the way, please feel free to let me know! My Discord is @ajthedragon345 . Thanks to Peaches and Rectilian for bouncing ideas off of, and Hzla and StaraptorOP for helping to compile and organize this data <3


Join the Discord for more info, patch updates, bug fixes, etc: https://discord.gg/Yf3GMQQNut
